# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Group Coordinator State and Protocol Handling

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the GroupCoordinator: the group metadata state machine (Empty, PreparingRebalance, CompletingRebalance, Stable, Dead), the JoinGroup/SyncGroup request handlers, and the heartbeat expiry detection.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

```json

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Perfect! I've successfully created a comprehensive analysis of the Apache Kafka GroupCoordinator implementation. Here's what I found:

## Summary

I identified **26 Java source files** in apache/kafka that implement the GroupCoordinator, including the group metadata state machine, JoinGroup/SyncGroup request handlers, and heartbeat expiry detection.

### Key Components:

1. **State Machines** - Three different state machines:
   - **ClassicGroupState**: EMPTY → PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE → DEAD
   - **ConsumerGroupState**: Modern protocol with EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD
   - **ShareGroupState**: Share-based subscriptions

2. **Core Interfaces & Implementations**:
   - **GroupCoordinator**: Interface defining all coordination methods (joinGroup, syncGroup, heartbeat)
   - **GroupCoordinatorService**: Concrete implementation handling request routing
   - **GroupCoordinatorShard**: Per-partition coordinator logic
   - **GroupMetadataManager**: State machine implementation with heartbeat expiry detection

3. **Request Handlers**:
   - JoinGroup processing: Validates members, triggers rebalancing
   - SyncGroup processing: Receives leader assignments, transitions to STABLE
   - Heartbeat processing: Reschedules expiry timeouts, detects member failures

4. **Heartbeat Expiry Detection**:
   - Members have session timeouts configured via GroupCoordinatorConfig
   - Each heartbeat reschedules the expiry timeout via `rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()`
   - When timeout fires, `expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()` is called
   - Removes member and triggers rebalance if needed

The complete analysis has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed information about file paths, key symbols, call chains, and implementation deta

STABLE: Group is stable, members send normal heartbeats\\n   - DEAD: Final state before group metadata cleanup\\n\\n2. **ConsumerGroupState** (in sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java): States for the modern consumer group protocol:\\n   - EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\\n\\n3. **ShareGroupState** and other modern group states in sg-evals/kafka--0753c489/group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### GroupCoordinator Interface\\n- **File**: group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java\\n- **Key Methods**:\\n  - `joinGroup()`: Handles JoinGroup requests for classic groups\\n  - `syncGroup()`: Handles SyncGroup requests for classic groups\\n  - `heartbeat()`: Processes heartbeat requests from classic group members\\n  - `consumerGroupHeartbeat()`: Modern consumer group heartbeat processing\\n  - `leaveGroup()`: Handles member departure\\n  - Additional methods for shares groups, streams groups, offset management\\n\\n### GroupCoordinatorService\\n- **File**: group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java\\n- **Purpose**: Concrete implementation of the GroupCoordinator interface\\n- **Key Methods**:\\n  - `joinGroup()`: Delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard with write operation\\n  - `syncGroup()`: Schedules sync group operations\\n  - Full lifecycle management of group coordination\\n\\n### GroupCoordinatorShard\\n- **File**: group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java\\n- **Purpose**: Handles per-partition coordination logic\\n- **Key Methods**:\\n  - `onJoinGroup()`: Processes join requests, handles state transitions\\n  - `onSyncGroup()`: Processes sync requests, manages member assignments\\n  - Implements CoordinatorShard interface for record-based state management\\n\\n### GroupMetadataManager\\n- **File**: group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java\\n- **Purpose**: Core state machine implementation for group metadata\\n- **Key Methods**:\\n  - `classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup()`: Handles join logic, member joins, rebalance preparation\\n  - `classicGroupSyncToClassicGroup()`: Handles sync logic, generates assignments, transitions to STABLE\\n  - `rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()`: Reschedules heartbeat expiry timeout\\n  - `expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()`: Called when heartbeat timeout expires, removes member, triggers rebalance\\n\\n## Group Implementations\\n\\n### ClassicGroup\\n- **File**: group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java\\n- **Purpose**: Represents a classic consumer group\\n- **Key Method**: `transitionTo()` - State machine transitions with validation\\n- Maintains members via ClassicGroupMember instances\\n- Manages generation IDs and leader election\\n\\n### ClassicGroupMember\\n- **File**: group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupMember.java\\n- **Purpose**: Represents individual member metadata\\n- Tracks session timeout, heartbeat metadata, supported protocols\\n- Maintains lastHeartbeatTime for expiry detection\\n\\n### ConsumerGroup\\n- **File**: group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java\\n- **Purpose**: Modern consumer group implementation\\n- Uses ConsumerGroupState enum for state management\\n- Extends ModernGroup base class\\n\\n### ShareGroup\\n- **File**: group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/ShareGroup.java\\n- **Purpose**: Share group coordination (Kafka Share API)\\n- State management for shared subscriptions\\n\\n## Heartbeat Expiry Detection\\n\\nThe heartbeat expiry mechanism works as follows:\\n\\n1. **Member Heartbeat Scheduling**: When a member joins or sends a heartbeat, `rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()` schedules a timeout using the member's sessionTimeoutMs\\n\\n2. **Timeout Expiry**: When the timeout fires, `expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat()` is called with the group ID and member ID\\n\\n3. **Expiry Handling**: The expiry handler:\\n   - Removes the member from the group\\n   - May trigger transition to PREPARING_REBALANCE if the group was STABLE\\n   - Or transitions to EMPTY if it was the last member\\n\\n4. **Configuration**: SessionTimeout values are defined in:\\n   - GroupCoordinatorConfig: Contains CLASSIC_GROUP_SESSION_TIMEOUT_MS settings\\n   - CommonClientConfigs: CLIENT-side session timeout configurations\\n\\n## Configuration and Metrics\\n\\n- **GroupCoordinatorConfig** (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorConfig.java): Central configuration for all group timeouts and limits\\n\\n- **GroupCoordinatorMetrics** and **GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard**: Track group state counts and other metrics\\n\\n## Key Files Summary\\n\\nThe implementation spans 26 Java source files organized in these directories:\\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/`: Core coordinator interfaces and implementations\\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/`: Classic group implementation\\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/`: Modern group implementations\\n- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/`: Metrics tracking\\n- `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/`: State enum definitions shared with clients\"\n}\n",
